namespace = magicka
#Set initial magicka.
character_event = {
	id = magicka.0
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	only_playable = yes
	ai = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_spellcaster = yes
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_character_modifier = magicka_counter } }
			set_magicka = yes
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = magicka_counter
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = magicka_counter
			}
			refresh_max_magicka = yes
		}
	}
}
#Magicka Regen
character_event = {
	id = magicka.1
	desc = magicka.1.d
	notification = yes
	picture = GFX_evt_mage
	
	only_playable = yes
	ai = no
	
	trigger = {
		is_spellcaster = yes
		has_character_modifier = magicka_counter
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		
		modifier = { factor = 0.80 any_artifact = { is_artifact_equipped = yes artifact_type = ring_of_erudite } }
		modifier = { factor = 0.80 any_artifact = { is_artifact_equipped = yes artifact_type = amulet_of_akatosh } }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 trait = dragonborn }
		modifier = { factor = 0.85 trait = dragonborn_descendant }
		modifier = { factor = 0.90 trait = lich }
		modifier = { factor = 0.90 trait = mane }
		modifier = { factor = 0.80 is_smart_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.20 is_dumb_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.15 has_mental_disorder_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.15 trait = skooma_addiction }
		modifier = { factor = 1.5 trait = chrondiasis }
		modifier = { factor = 1.25 has_severe_disability_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.15 has_medium_disability_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.05 has_minor_disability_trigger = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 1.25 has_disease_trigger = yes NOT = { trait = chrondiasis} }
		modifier = { factor = 0.9 has_magicka_regen_0 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.85 has_magicka_regen_1 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.8 has_magicka_regen_2 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 has_magicka_regen_3 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.7 has_magicka_regen_4 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.65 has_magicka_regen_5 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.6 has_magicka_regen_6 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.55 has_magicka_regen_7 = yes }
		modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_magicka_regen_8 = yes }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		regen_magicka_effect = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 999503
	hide_window = yes
	min_age = 16

	trigger = {
		ai = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = timer_boost_morale_defence }
				OR = { trait = spell_boost_morale_defence_1 trait = spell_boost_morale_defence_2 trait = spell_boost_morale_defence_3 }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = timer_boost_morale_offence }
				OR = { trait = spell_boost_morale_offence_1 trait = spell_boost_morale_offence_2 trait = spell_boost_morale_offence_3 }

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = timer_boost_morale_defence }

#600000-6999999
#Spell System by Novacat

character_event = {
	id = 600000
	desc = EVTDESC600000
	picture = GFX_evt_mage
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA600000
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 1 }
			OR = {
				is_mage = yes
				has_court_mage = yes
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_1
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_1 = yes
				
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_1
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_2
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_3
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_fertility_1
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_fertility_2
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_fertility_3

				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_diplomacy_2
				remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_diplomacy_3

#Character Modifiers#

character_event = {
	id = 600001
	desc = EVTDESC600001
	picture = GFX_evt_mage
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA600001
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 3 }
			OR = {
				is_mage = yes
				has_court_mage = yes
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_3
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_3 = yes
				
				FROM = {
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_1
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_2
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_3
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = spell_fortify_health_1
						duration = 3650
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				opinion = {
					who = FROMFROM
					modifier = opinion_blessed_me
					months = 120
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB600001
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 9 }
			OR = {
				trait = mage_2
				trait = mage_3
				is_master_mage = yes
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_9
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_9 = yes
				
				FROM = {
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_1
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_2
					remove_character_modifier = spell_fortify_health_3
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = spell_fortify_health_2
						duration = 3650
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {

character_event = {
	id = 600100
	desc = EVTDESC600100
	picture = GFX_evt_mage
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
		set_variable = { which = roll_variable which = birth_seed }
		set_variable = { which = succ_chance value = 184.5 } #50% chance of success.
		set_variable = { which = modulus value = 369 }
		multiply_variable = { which = roll_variable which = global_seed }
		
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = roll_variable which = modulus }
			}
			subtract_variable = { which = roll_variable which = modulus }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA600100
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 60 }
			is_immortal = no
			NOT = { trait = undead }
			trait = mage_5
		}
		wealth = -100
		piety = -100
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_60
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_60 = yes
				if = { #Success
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = roll_variable which = succ_chance }
					}
					character_event = { id = 600101 }
				}
				else = { #Failure
					character_event = { id = 600102 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB600100
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	after = { #Halt! Who goes there?
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = roll_variable value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = succ_chance value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = modulus value = 0 }
		}
	}
}

	}

			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 55 }
			NOT = { culture = altmer }
			trait = mage_5
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_55
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_55 = yes
				add_trait = disabler

				set_graphical_culture = altmer
				culture = altmer
				add_altmer_trait = yes
				add_trait = impure_altmer
				set_character_flag = race_changer
				remove_congenital_traits_racechange = yes
				assign_random_congenital_racechange = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB600123
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { trait = disabler }
			remove_trait = disabler
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA600124
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 55 }
			NOT = { culture = bosmer }
			trait = mage_5
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_55
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_55 = yes
				add_trait = disabler
				
				remove_racial_trait = yes
				set_graphical_culture = bosmer
				culture = bosmer
				add_bosmer_trait = yes
				set_character_flag = race_changer
				remove_congenital_traits_racechange = yes
				assign_random_congenital_racechange = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB600124
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { trait = disabler }
			remove_trait = disabler
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA600141
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 3 }
			OR = {
				is_mage = yes
				has_court_mage = yes
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_3
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_3 = yes
				
				FROM = {
					remove_character_modifier = spell_drain_health_1
					remove_character_modifier = spell_drain_health_2
					remove_character_modifier = spell_drain_health_3
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = spell_drain_health_1
						duration = 3650
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = { 
				limit = { 
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
				}
				opinion = {
					who = FROMFROM
					modifier = opinion_cursed_me

	id = 600165

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = casting_spell
	}

		name = EVTOPTA600165
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = magicka_current value = 30 }
			trait = necromancer
			is_master_mage = yes
		}
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
		custom_tooltip = { text = MAGICKA_COST_30
			hidden_tooltip = {
				spell_cost_30 = yes
				
				random_list = {
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = tuberculosis } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = typhoid_fever } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = typhus } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = measles } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = small_pox } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = syphilis } } }
					10 = { FROM = { location = { spawn_disease = swamp_rot } } }
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			owner = {
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					}
					opinion = {
						who = FROMFROM
						modifier = opinion_cursed_my_lands
						months = 360
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTD600165
		clr_character_flag = casting_spell
	}
